          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





The function `CountPages` is a recursive function|2| in `pdfium/core/fpdfapi/parser/cpdf_document.cpp` file.



<span class="line"><!---->The function `CountPages` is a recursive function|2| in `pdfium/core/fpdfapi/parser/cpdf_document.cpp` file.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If the Pages Object has enough `Kids` and the Kid Object must have `Kids` key. 



<span class="line"><!---->If the Pages Object has enough `Kids` and the Kid Object must have `Kids` key. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





And we can control the Kid Object `Count` value |1|.The Kid Object `Count` value can be 0xFFFFE < CPDF_Document::kPageMaxNum|1|.



<span class="line"><!---->And we can control the Kid Object `Count` value |1|.The Kid Object `Count` value can be 0xFFFFE &lt; CPDF_Document::kPageMaxNum|1|.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





int CountPages(RetainPtr<CPDF_Dictionary> pPages,



<span class="line"><!---->int CountPages(RetainPtr&lt;CPDF_Dictionary&gt; pPages,<!----></span>



<br>





               std::set<RetainPtr<CPDF_Dictionary>>* visited_pages) {



<span class="line"><!---->               std::set&lt;RetainPtr&lt;CPDF_Dictionary&gt;&gt;* visited_pages) {<!----></span>



<br>





  int count = pPages->GetIntegerFor("Count");



<span class="line"><!---->  int count = pPages-&gt;GetIntegerFor("Count");<!----></span>



<br>





  if (count > 0 && count < CPDF_Document::kPageMaxNum)



<span class="line"><!---->  if (count &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; count &lt; CPDF_Document::kPageMaxNum)<!----></span>



<br>





    return count;//***1***



<span class="line"><!---->    return count;//***1***<!----></span>



<br>





  RetainPtr<CPDF_Array> pKidList = pPages->GetMutableArrayFor("Kids");



<span class="line"><!---->  RetainPtr&lt;CPDF_Array&gt; pKidList = pPages-&gt;GetMutableArrayFor("Kids");<!----></span>



<br>





  if (!pKidList)



<span class="line"><!---->  if (!pKidList)<!----></span>



<br>





    return 0;



<span class="line"><!---->    return 0;<!----></span>



<br>





  count = 0;



<span class="line"><!---->  count = 0;<!----></span>



<br>





  for (size_t i = 0; i < pKidList->size(); i++) {



<span class="line"><!---->  for (size_t i = 0; i &lt; pKidList-&gt;size(); i++) {<!----></span>



<br>





    RetainPtr<CPDF_Dictionary> pKid = pKidList->GetMutableDictAt(i);



<span class="line"><!---->    RetainPtr&lt;CPDF_Dictionary&gt; pKid = pKidList-&gt;GetMutableDictAt(i);<!----></span>



<br>





    if (!pKid || pdfium::Contains(*visited_pages, pKid))



<span class="line"><!---->    if (!pKid || pdfium::Contains(*visited_pages, pKid))<!----></span>



<br>





      continue;



<span class="line"><!---->      continue;<!----></span>



<br>





    if (pKid->KeyExist("Kids")) {



<span class="line"><!---->    if (pKid-&gt;KeyExist("Kids")) {<!----></span>



<br>





      // Use |visited_pages| to help detect circular references of pages.



<span class="line"><!---->      // Use |visited_pages| to help detect circular references of pages.<!----></span>



<br>





      ScopedSetInsertion<RetainPtr<CPDF_Dictionary>> local_add(visited_pages,



<span class="line"><!---->      ScopedSetInsertion&lt;RetainPtr&lt;CPDF_Dictionary&gt;&gt; local_add(visited_pages,<!----></span>



<br>





                                                               pKid);



<span class="line"><!---->                                                               pKid);<!----></span>



<br>





      count += CountPages(std::move(pKid), visited_pages);//***2***



<span class="line"><!---->      count += CountPages(std::move(pKid), visited_pages);//***2***<!----></span>



<br>





    } else {



<span class="line"><!---->    } else {<!----></span>



<br>





      // This page is a leaf node.



<span class="line"><!---->      // This page is a leaf node.<!----></span>



<br>





      count++;



<span class="line"><!---->      count++;<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





  pPages->SetNewFor<CPDF_Number>("Count", count);



<span class="line"><!---->  pPages-&gt;SetNewFor&lt;CPDF_Number&gt;("Count", count);<!----></span>



<br>





  return count;



<span class="line"><!---->  return count;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
